Parsing [sent. 430 len. 19]: Mr and Mrs Chester returned from their visit to Hurst Manor with somewhat different accounts of the establishment .
Parsing [sent. 431 len. 24]: The father was delighted with all he had seen , thought the arrangements excellent , and Miss Bruce a charming and lovable woman .

Parsing [sent. 436 len. 91]: The big , new box with her initials on the side ; the dressing-bag with its dainty fittings ; the writing-case and workbox ; the miniature medicine chest stocked with domestic remedies , in case she should feel feverish or chilled , have earache , toothache , or headache ; be threatened with sore throat or swollen glands -- they were all new possessions , and as such afforded acute satisfaction , for though the wardrobe list was disappointingly short , there were at least no restrictions as to quality .
Parsing [sent. 437 len. 34]: When the key was turned in her box Rhoda heaved a sigh of satisfaction in the confidence that not one of the two hundred girls could possess a better equipment than her own .

Parsing [sent. 3357 len. 5]: MRS. CHESTER 'S PLAN .
